style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">pk-cpa-R&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.83em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>and so <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></mrow></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\mathrm{cpa}-\mathrm{L}} \approx \mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\mathrm{cpa}-\mathrm{R}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">c</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">a</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">L</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">c</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">a</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">R</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>The reason this proof goes through for public-key encryption but not symmetric-key encryption is that <em>anyone can encrypt</em> in a public-key scheme. In a symmetric-key scheme, it is not possible to generate encryptions without the key. But in a public-key scheme, the encryption key is public.</p>
<p>In more detail, the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mtext>hyb-&nbsp;</mtext><mi>h</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text {hyb- } h}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">hyb-&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">h</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> library can indeed obtain <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">p</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span></span> from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mtext>pk-ots&nbsp;</mtext><mo>−</mo><mo>⋆</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text {pk-ots }-\star .}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">pk-ots&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">⋆</span><span class="mord mtight">.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. It therefore has enough information to perform the encryptions for all calls to CHALLENGE. Indeed, you can think of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mtext>hyb-&nbsp;</mtext><mn>0</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text {hyb- } 0}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">hyb-&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> as doing everything that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>pk-cpa-L&nbsp;</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text {pk-cpa-L }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">pk-cpa-L&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> does, even though it doesn’t know the secret key. We let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mtext>hyb-&nbsp;</mtext><mi>h</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text {hyb- } h}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">hyb-&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">h</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> designate the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>h</mi><mtext>th&nbsp;</mtext></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h^{\text {th }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.849108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">th&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> call to CHALLENGE as a special one to be handled by <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">t</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mo>⋆</mo></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\mathrm{ots}-\star} .</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">o</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">t</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">s</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">⋆</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span> This allows us to change the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>h</mi><mtext>th&nbsp;</mtext></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">h^{\text {th }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.849108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">h</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">th&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> encryption from using <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>m</mi><mi>L</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m_{L}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">m</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">L</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>m</mi><mi>R</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m_{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58056em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">m</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.328331em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 id="elgamal-encryption">15.3 ElGamal Encryption</h2>
<p>ElGamal encryption is a public-key encryption scheme that is based on DHKA.</p>
<p><strong>Construction 15.6 (ElGamal)</strong><br>
The public parameters are a choice of cyclic group <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{G}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">G</span></span></span></span></span></span> with n elements and generator <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>g</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left left left left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">M</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">C</mi><mo>=</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><munder accentunder="true"><mtext>KeyGen:</mtext><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="double-struck">Z</mi><mi>n</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>B</mi><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>return</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mi>b</mi></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><munder accentunder="true"><mrow><mtext>Dec</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>return&nbsp;</mtext><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>B</mi><mi>a</mi></msup><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|llll|} \hline
\begin{array}{l}
\mathcal{M}=\mathbb{G}\\
\mathcal{C}=\mathbb{G}^2
\end{array}
&amp;
\begin{array}{l}
\underline{\text{KeyGen:}}\\
\quad sk:=a\leftarrow\mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad pk:=A:=g^a\\
\quad\text{return} (pk,sk)
\end{array}
&amp;
\begin{array}{l}
\underline{\text{Enc}(A,M\in\mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad b\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad B:=g^b\\
\quad\text{return} (B,M\cdot A^b)
\end{array}
&amp;
\begin{array}{l}
\underline{\text{Dec}(a,(B,X)):}\\
\quad \text{return} \ X(B^a)^{-1}
\end{array}\\\hline
\end{array}

style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Dec</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.45em;"><span 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.814108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.35em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="vertical-separator" style="height: 7.2em; vertical-align: -3.35em;"></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -2.5em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 5.85em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -9.7em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 5.85em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.35em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>The scheme satisfies correctness, since for all <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> :<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Dec</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>s</mi><mi>k</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Enc</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Dec</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>s</mi><mi>k</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mi>b</mi></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mi>b</mi></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi>a</mi></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mi>M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{aligned}
\operatorname{Dec}(s k, \operatorname{Enc}(p k, M)) &amp;=\operatorname{Dec}\left(s k,\left(g^{b}, M \cdot A^{b}\right)\right) \\
&amp;=\left(M \cdot A^{b}\right)\left(\left(g^{b}\right)^{a}\right)^{-1} \\
&amp;=M \cdot\left(g^{a b}\right)\left(g^{a b}\right)^{-1}=M .
\end{aligned}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 5.62625em; vertical-align: -2.56313em;"></span><span <h3 id="security">Security</h3>
<p>Imagine an adversary who is interested in attacking an ElGamal scheme. This adversary sees the public key <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>a</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A=g^{a}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.858832em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">a</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and a ciphertext <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>M</mi><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow></msup><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\left(g^{b}, M g^{a b}\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.20001em; vertical-align: -0.35001em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size1">(</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">a</span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size1">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> go by. Intuitively, the Decisional Diffie-Hellman assumption says that the value <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g^{a b}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04355em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">a</span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> looks random, even to someone who has seen <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>a</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g^{a}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.858832em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">a</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g^{b}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04355em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. Thus, the message <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span></span></span></span></span> is masked with a pseudorandom group element-as we’ve seen before, this is a lot like masking the message with a random pad as in one-time pad. The only change here is that instead of the xor operation, we are using the group operation in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{G}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">G</span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>More formally, we can prove the security of ElGamal under the DDH assumption:</p>
<p><strong>Claim 15.7</strong><br>
If the DDH assumption in group G is true, then ElGamal in group <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{G}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">G</span></span></span></span></span></span> is C P A <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Φ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\varPhi</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">Φ</span></span></span></span></span></span> -secure.</p>
<p><strong>Proof</strong><br>
It suffices to show that ElGamal has pseudorandom ciphertexts when the calling program sees only a single ciphertext. In other words, we will show that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mtext>-ots</mtext><mi>Φ</mi><mo>−</mo><mtext>real</mtext></mrow></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mtext>ots</mtext><mi>φ</mi><mtext>-rand&nbsp;</mtext></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}\text {-ots}\varPhi-\text{real}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\text {ots}\varphi\text{-rand }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">-ots</span></span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">Φ</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">real</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ots</span></span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">φ</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">-rand&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, where these libraries are the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mo>⋆</mo></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\mathrm{cpas}-\star}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">c</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">a</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">s</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">⋆</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> libraries from Definition 15.2 but with the singleciphertext restriction used in Definition 15.4. It is left as an exercise to show that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mtext>-ots</mtext><mi>Φ</mi><mo>−</mo><mtext>real</mtext></mrow></msub><mo>≈</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mtext>ots</mtext><mi>φ</mi><mtext>-rand&nbsp;</mtext></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}\text {-ots}\varPhi-\text{real}}\approx\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\text {ots}\varphi\text{-rand }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">-ots</span></span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">Φ</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">real</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ots</span></span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">φ</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">-rand&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> implies CPA<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Φ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\varPhi</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">Φ</span></span></span></span></span></span> security (which in turn implies CPA security); the proof is very similar to that of Claim 15.5 .</p>
<p>The sequence of hybrid libraries is given below:<br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em" rowlines="solid none none none none none none none none none none none"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mtext>pk-ots</mtext><mi>Φ</mi><mo>−</mo><mtext>real</mtext></mrow></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="double-struck">Z</mi><mi>n</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>a</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mtext>count</mtext><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><munder accentunder="true"><mtext>GETPK():</mtext><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mrow><mtext>return&nbsp;</mtext><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mi>A</mi></mstyle></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><munder accentunder="true"><mrow><mtext>QUERY</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>count&nbsp;:&nbsp;count+1</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>if&nbsp;count</mtext><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>:</mo><mtext>&nbsp;return&nbsp;null</mtext></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>b</mi><mo>←</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="double-struck">Z</mi><mi>n</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>B</mi><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>return</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
\qquad \quad \mathcal{L}_{\text{pk-ots}\varPhi-\text{real}} \\ \hline
a\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
A:=g^a\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad b\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad B:=g^b\\
\quad X:=M\cdot A^b\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 23.45em; vertical-align: -11.45em;"></span><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: 4.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: 7.65em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.26em;"></span><span <p>The starting point is the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mtext>pk-ots</mtext><mi>Φ</mi><mo>−</mo><mtext>real</mtext></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{pk-ots}\varPhi-\text{real}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">pk-ots</span></span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">Φ</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">real</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> library, shown here with the details of ElGamal filled in.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>←</mo><msub><mi accentunder="true"><mtext>GETPK():</mtext><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>return</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
a\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n;b\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
A:=g^a;B:=g^b;C:=A^b\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad X:=M\cdot C\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 18.05em; vertical-align: -8.75em;"></span><span mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>The main body of QUERY computes some intermediate values <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A^b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.849108em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> . But since those lines are only reachable one time, it does not change anything to precompute them at initialization time.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable displaystyle="false"><mrow><mtext>count</mtext><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><munder accentunder="true"><mtext>GETPK():</mtext><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose><mspace width="1em"></mspace><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable rowspacing="0.6599999999999999em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em" rowlines="solid none none"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="2em"></mspace><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>dh-real</mtext></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
(A,B,C)\leftarrow \text{DHQUERY()}\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad X:=M\cdot C\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}
\quad
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
\qquad\mathcal{L}_{\text{dh-real}}\\\hline
\text{DHQUERY()}\\
\quad a,b\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad \text{return} (g^a,g^b,g^{ab})\\\hline
\end{array}

<p>We can factor out the generation of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A, B, C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.87777em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">A</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></span> in terms of the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>dh-real</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{dh-real}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">dh-real</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> library from the Decisional Diffie-Hellman security definition (Definition 14.5).</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable \def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
(A,B,C)\leftarrow \text{DHQUERY()}\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad X:=M\cdot C\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}
\quad
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
\qquad\mathcal{L}_{\text{dh-rand}}\\\hline
\text{DHQUERY()}\\
\quad a,b,c\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad \text{return} (g^a,g^b,g^{c})\\\hline
\end{array}

<p>Applying the security of DDH, we can replace <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mtext>dh-real</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\text{dh-real}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; <p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable accentunder="true"><mtext>GETPK():</mtext><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></munder></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mtext>return</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
(a,b,c)\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
A:=g^a;B:=g^b;C:=g^c\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad X:=M\cdot C\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}

<p>The call to DHQUERY has been in lined.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable></menclose></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
a\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
A:=g^a\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad b,c\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad B:=g^b:C:=g^c\\
\quad X:=M\cdot C\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}

<p>As before, since the main body of QUERY is only reachable once, we can move the choice of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></span> into that subroutine instead of at initialization time.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable \def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|l|} \hline
\qquad \quad \mathcal{L}_{\text{pk-ots}\varPhi-\text{rand}} \\ \hline
a\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
A:=g^a\\
\text{count}=0\\
\underline{\text{GETPK():}}\\
\quad \text{return $A$}\\
\underline{\text{QUERY}(M\in \mathbb{G}):}\\
\quad \text{count : count+1}\\
\quad \text{if count} &gt; 1:\ \text{return null}\\
\quad b,x\leftarrow \mathbb{Z}_n\\
\quad B:=g^b:X:=g^x\\
\quad \text{return} (B,X)\\\hline
\end{array}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 21.65em; vertical-align: -10.55em;"></span><span class="" style="top: -22.3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 13.05em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span><span class="" style="top: -24.1em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 13.05em;"></span><span class="hline" style="border-bottom-width: 0.05em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 10.55em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>When <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span></span></span></span></span> is sampled uniformly from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="double-struck">Z</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{Z}n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">Z</span></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span>, the expression <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B = g^b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04355em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is a uniformly distributed element of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{G}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">G</span></span></span></span></span></span>. Also recall that when <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></span> is a uniformly distributed element of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{G}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68889em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">G</span></span></span></span></span></span>, then <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M \cdot C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></span> is uniformly distributed — this is analogous to the one-time pad property (see Exercise 2.5). Applying this change gives the library to the left.</p>
<p>In the final hybrid, the response to QUERY is a pair of uniformly distributed group elements <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(B, X) .</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span> Hence that library is exactly <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="script">L</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mtext>&nbsp;ots&nbsp;</mtext><mi>Φ</mi><mtext>&nbsp;-rand&nbsp;</mtext></mrow></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{pk}-\text { ots } \varPhi \text { -rand }},</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">L</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">p</span><span class="mord mathrm mtight">k</span></span><span class="mbin mtight">−</span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">&nbsp;ots&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">Φ</span></span><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">&nbsp;-rand&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span> as desired.</p>
<h3 id="hybrid-encryption">Hybrid Encryption</h3>
<p>As a rule, public-key encryption schemes are much more computationally expensive than symmetric-key schemes. Taking ElGamal as a representative example, computing <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>g</mi><mi>b</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g^{b}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.04355em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.849108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">b</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> in a cryptographically secure cyclic group is considerably more expensive than one evaluation of AES. As the plaintext data increases in length, the difference in cost between public-key and symmetric-key techniques only gets worse.</p>
<p>A clever way to minimize the cost of public-key cryptography is to use a method called <strong>hybrid encryption</strong>. The idea is to use the expensive public-key scheme to encrypt a <em>temporary key</em> for a symmetric-key scheme. Then use the temporary key to (cheaply) encrypt the large plaintext data.</p>
<p>To decrypt, one can use the decryption key of the public-key scheme to obtain the temporary key. Then the temporary key can be used to decrypt the main payload.</p>
<p><strong>Construction 15.8 (Hybrid Enc)</strong><br>
Let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Σ</mi><mtext>pub&nbsp;</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Sigma_{\text {pub }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">pub&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> be a public-key encryption scheme, and let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Σ</mi><mtext>sym&nbsp;</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Sigma_{\text {sym }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">sym&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> be a symmetric-key encryption scheme, where <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Σ</mi><mtext>sym.&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mi mathvariant="script">K</mi><mo>⊆</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Σ</mi><mtext>pub.&nbsp;</mtext></msub><mi mathvariant="script">M</mi><mo>−</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Sigma_{\text {sym. }} \mathcal{K} \subseteq \Sigma_{\text {pub. }} \mathcal{M}-</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">sym.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.01445em;">K</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊆</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.969438em; vertical-align: -0.286108em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">pub.&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.286108em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal">M</span></span><span class="mord">−</span></span></span></span></span> that is, the public-key scheme is capable of encrypting keys of the symmetric-key scheme.</p>
<p>Then we define <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Σ</mi><mtext>hvb&nbsp;</mtext></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Sigma_{\text {hvb }}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.336108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">hvb&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> to be the following construction:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><menclose notation="top bottom left right"><mtable \def\arraystretch{1.5}
\begin{array}{|llll|} \hline
\begin{array}{l}
\mathcal{M}=\Sigma_{sym}.\mathcal{M}\\
\mathcal{C}=\Sigma_{pub}.\mathcal{C}\times \Sigma_{sym}.\mathcal{C}\\\\
\underline{\text{KeyGen:}}\\
\quad (pk,sk)\leftarrow\Sigma_{pub}.\text{KeyGen}\\
\quad\text{return} (pk,sk)
\end{array}
&amp;
\begin{array}{l}
\underline{\text{Enc}(pk,m):}\\
\quad tk\leftarrow \Sigma_{sym}.\text{KeyGen}\\
\quad c_{pub}\leftarrow \Sigma_{pub}.\text{Enc}(tk,m)\\
\quad\text{return} (c_{pub},c_{sym})\\
\underline{\text{Dec}(sk,(c_{pub},c_{sym})):}\\
\quad tk:=\Sigma_{pub}.\text{Dec}(sk,c_{pub})\\
\quad\text{return}\ \Sigma_{sym}.\text{Dec}(tk,c_{sym})
\end{array}\\\hline
\end{array}

class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 6.05em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="vertical-separator"
